When the threshold is exceeded, `G1Policy::initiate_conc_mark()` is called, which sets the collector state (via `g1CollectorState.cpp`) to `in_concurrent_start_gc=true` and clears `initiate_conc_mark_if_possible`. This signals the `G1ConcurrentMarkThread` (in `g1ConcurrentMarkThread.cpp`) to begin a new marking cycle. The cycle starts with `G1ConcurrentMark::concurrent_cycle_start()` followed by `G1ConcurrentMark::mark_from_roots()` which does the actual concurrent tracing. The `G1ConcurrentMark` object itself is constructed and initialized in `g1CollectedHeap.cpp`. VM operations for initiating concurrent marking safepoints are in `g1VMOperations.cpp`.\\n\\n## 2. SATB Marking Queue Processing\\n\\nThe Snapshot-At-The-Beginning (SATB) write barrier is implemented across:\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1BarrierSet.cpp` — `G1BarrierSet::write_ref_array_pre_work()` and related methods intercept reference writes. When the SATB queue is active during concurrent marking, the pre-value of the overwritten reference is enqueued into the thread-local `SATBMarkQueue`.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1BarrierSetRuntime.cpp` — runtime stub `write_ref_field_pre_entry()` for compiled code paths that invokes `enqueue_known_active()` to log the old reference value.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/shared/satbMarkQueue.cpp` — base `SATBMarkQueue` and `SATBMarkQueueSet` classes. Buffers fill up during mutation and become 'completed buffers' for concurrent processing.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1SATBMarkQueueSet.cpp` — `G1SATBMarkQueueSet` extends the base with G1-specific filtering (`G1SATBMarkQueueFilterFn`) to exclude already-marked or young-gen references. During the Remark STW pause, `g1ConcurrentMark.cpp` contains `G1RemarkThreadsClosure` which flushes per-thread SATB queues so all remaining pre-values are processed before marking concludes.\\n\\n## 3. Remembered Set Scanning\\n\\nThe remembered set (remset) infrastructure is implemented in:\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSet.cpp` — central `G1RemSet` class. `prepare_for_scan_heap_roots()` initializes the `G1RemSetScanState`; `scan_heap_roots()` iterates dirty card ranges and scans for cross-region references pointing into the collection set. The `G1RemSetScanState` inner class manages which regions have dirty cards to scan.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1HeapRegionRemSet.cpp` — per-region remembered set (`G1HeapRegionRemSet`) that tracks which other regions have pointers into a given region.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSet.cpp` — the card-set data structure (`G1CardSet`) backing each region's remembered set using a HOWL (Hierarchical Or With Lists) structure.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSetTrackingPolicy.cpp` — decides which regions need remset tracking (`update_at_allocate`, `update_at_free`).\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentRebuildAndScrub.cpp` — concurrently rebuilds and scrubs remembered sets after a marking cycle completes.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1DirtyCardQueue.cpp` — the dirty card queue that feeds concurrent refinement threads (`g1ConcurrentRefine.cpp`) which keep remsets up to date between GC pauses.\\n\\n## 4. Mixed Collection Region Selection\\n\\nAfter concurrent marking completes, old-gen regions become candidates for mixed GC collections:\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetChooser.cpp` — `G1CollectionSetChooser::build()` is invoked post-marking to scan all old-gen regions, compute reclaimable bytes from the marking liveness data, sort regions by GC efficiency (reclaimable bytes per cost), and populate `G1CollectionSetCandidates`.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.cpp` — `G1CollectionSetCandidates` maintains the sorted list of candidate old-gen regions across marking groups and retained regions, and tracks membership in the collection set.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSet.cpp` — `G1CollectionSet::finalize_old_part()` selects the actual set of old-gen regions for a mixed GC pause, constrained by the remaining pause time budget, pulling from candidates in efficiency order.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1YoungCollector.cpp` — `calculate_collection_set()` orchestrates collection set construction calling `finalize_initial_collection_set()` which in turn calls `finalize_old_part()` for mixed GC pauses.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1YoungGCPostEvacuateTasks.cpp` — post-GC tasks handle retained regions and re-sort candidates after each mixed collection.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1Policy.cpp` — `G1Policy::candidates()` exposes the collection set candidates, and policy logic in `about_to_start_mixed_phase()` gates transition into the mixed collection phase.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":3,"cache_creation_input_tokens":374,"cache_read_input_tokens":44953,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":374,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"afe17ba9-4ecb-4cec-a86f-10d7e5f775d8","uuid":"bb6607fd-3911-4517-8582-63db2ddff423"}

G1ConcurrentMark Start Trigger\\n\\nThe decision to initiate concurrent marking is made in `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1Policy.cpp`. When the threshold is exceeded, `G1Policy::initiate_conc_mark()` is called, which sets the collector state (via `g1CollectorState.cpp`) to `in_concurrent_start_gc=true` and clears `initiate_conc_mark_if_possible`. This signals the `G1ConcurrentMarkThread` (in `g1ConcurrentMarkThread.cpp`) to begin a new marking cycle. The cycle starts with `G1ConcurrentMark::concurrent_cycle_start()` followed by `G1ConcurrentMark::mark_from_roots()` which does the actual concurrent tracing. The `G1ConcurrentMark` object itself is constructed and initialized in `g1CollectedHeap.cpp`. VM operations for initiating concurrent marking safepoints are in `g1VMOperations.cpp`.\\n\\n## 2. SATB Marking Queue Processing\\n\\nThe Snapshot-At-The-Beginning (SATB) write barrier is implemented across:\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1BarrierSet.cpp` — `G1BarrierSet::write_ref_array_pre_work()` and related methods intercept reference writes. When the SATB queue is active during concurrent marking, the pre-value of the overwritten reference is enqueued into the thread-local `SATBMarkQueue`.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1BarrierSetRuntime.cpp` — runtime stub `write_ref_field_pre_entry()` for compiled code paths that invokes `enqueue_known_active()` to log the old reference value.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/shared/satbMarkQueue.cpp` — base `SATBMarkQueue` and `SATBMarkQueueSet` classes. Remembered Set Scanning\\n\\nThe remembered set (remset) infrastructure is implemented in:\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSet.cpp` — central `G1RemSet` class. `prepare_for_scan_heap_roots()` initializes the `G1RemSetScanState`; `scan_heap_roots()` iterates dirty card ranges and scans for cross-region references pointing into the collection set. The `G1RemSetScanState` inner class manages which regions have dirty cards to scan.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1HeapRegionRemSet.cpp` — per-region remembered set (`G1HeapRegionRemSet`) that tracks which other regions have pointers into a given region.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CardSet.cpp` — the card-set data structure (`G1CardSet`) backing each region's remembered set using a HOWL (Hierarchical Or With Lists) structure.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1RemSetTrackingPolicy.cpp` — decides which regions need remset tracking (`update_at_allocate`, `update_at_free`).\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1ConcurrentRebuildAndScrub.cpp` — concurrently rebuilds and scrubs remembered sets after a marking cycle completes.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1DirtyCardQueue.cpp` — the dirty card queue that feeds concurrent refinement threads (`g1ConcurrentRefine.cpp`) which keep remsets up to date between GC pauses.\\n\\n## 4. Mixed Collection Region Selection\\n\\nAfter concurrent marking completes, old-gen regions become candidates for mixed GC collections:\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetChooser.cpp` — `G1CollectionSetChooser::build()` is invoked post-marking to scan all old-gen regions, compute reclaimable bytes from the marking liveness data, sort regions by GC efficiency (reclaimable bytes per cost), and populate `G1CollectionSetCandidates`.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSetCandidates.cpp` — `G1CollectionSetCandidates` maintains the sorted list of candidate old-gen regions across marking groups and retained regions, and tracks membership in the collection set.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1CollectionSet.cpp` — `G1CollectionSet::finalize_old_part()` selects the actual set of old-gen regions for a mixed GC pause, constrained by the remaining pause time budget, pulling from candidates in efficiency order.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1YoungCollector.cpp` — `calculate_collection_set()` orchestrates collection set construction calling `finalize_initial_collection_set()` which in turn calls `finalize_old_part()` for mixed GC pauses.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1YoungGCPostEvacuateTasks.cpp` — post-GC tasks handle retained regions and re-sort candidates after each mixed collection.\\n- `src/hotspot/share/gc/g1/g1Policy.cpp` — `G1Policy::candidates()` exposes the collection set candidates, and policy logic in `about_to_start_mixed_phase()` gates transition into the mixed collection phase.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
